──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n@Composable\nprivate fun AccountRow(\n    account: 
UserProfile,\n    isCurrent: Boolean,\n    onClick: () -> Unit,\n) {\n    Row(\n        modifier = Modifier\n          
  .fillMaxWidth()\n            .clip(RoundedCornerShape(16.dp))\n            .background(\n                if

        )\n            .clickable(onClick = onClick)\n            .padding(horizontal = 14.dp, vertical = 10.dp),\n    
    verticalAlignment = Alignment.CenterVertically,\n        horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.spacedBy(14.dp)\n    
) {\n        AvatarCircle(\n            photoUrl = account.photoUrl,\n            displayName = account.displayName,\n 
           size = 40.dp,\n            textStyle = MaterialTheme.typography.titleSmall,\n            highlightColor = 
if (isCurrent) MaterialTheme.colorScheme.primary else null\n        )\n\n        Column(modifier = 
Modifier.weight(1f)) {\n            Text(\n                text = account.displayName,\n                style = 
MaterialTheme.typography.bodyMedium,\n                fontWeight = if (isCurrent) FontWeight.SemiBold else 
FontWeight.Normal,\n                color = if (isCurrent)\n                    
MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onPrimaryContainer\n                else\n                    
MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurface,\n                maxLines = 1\n            )\n            Text(\n                
text = account.email,\n                style = MaterialTheme.typography.labelSmall,\n                color = if 
(isCurrent)\n                    MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onPrimaryContainer.copy(alpha = 0.65f)\n                
else\n                    MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurface.copy(alpha = 0.5f),\n                maxLines = 1\n      
      )\n        }\n\n        if (isCurrent) {\n            Box(\n                modifier = Modifier\n                
    .size(8.dp)\n                    .background(MaterialTheme.colorScheme.primary, CircleShape)\n            )\n      
  }\n    }\n}\n\n// ── Shared: Avatar circle ────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n@Composable\nfun 
AvatarCircle(\n    photoUrl: String?,\n    displayName: String,\n    size: Dp,\n    textStyle: 
androidx.compose.ui.text.TextStyle,\n    highlightColor: Color? = null,\n) {\n    val bgColor = highlightColor ?: 
MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurface\n\n    if (!photoUrl.isNullOrEmpty()) {\n        AsyncImage(\n            model = 
photoUrl,\n            contentDescription = displayName,\n            modifier = Modifier\n                
.size(size)\n                .clip(CircleShape)\n        )\n    } else {\n        Box(\n            modifier = 
Modifier\n                .size(size)\n                .clip(CircleShape)\n                .background(bgColor),\n     
       contentAlignment = Alignment.Center\n        ) {\n            Text(\n                text = 
displayName.firstOrNull()?.uppercase() ?: \"?\",\n                style = textStyle,\n                fontWeight = 
FontWeight.Bold,\n                color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.surface\n            )\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n//
